    function checkAndRemoveClass() {
        const htmlTag = document.documentElement; // Select the <html> tag

        // Check if the <html> tag does NOT have the specified style
        if (htmlTag.style.height !== "100%" || htmlTag.style.overflow !== "hidden") {

	<section class="section-services-about bg-cream text-center section-padding">
<div class="container">
<div class="row justify-content-center">
<div class="section-content text-center">
<h2><span id="Whats_included_in_seasonal_air_conditioning_services_in_Tucson">What’s included in seasonal air conditioning services in Tucson?</span></h2>
</div>
<div class="col-lg-9">
<div class="section-heading">
<p>Your AC is an essential part of comfort in your home. Many homeowners do not give it much thought until it stops working as well as it used to. Instead of waiting for your AC to break down and need serious repairs. You can save yourself time and money by getting seasonal Air Conditioning Service. Call Intelligent Design <a href="https://www.idesignac.com/air-conditioning/">Air Conditioning</a>, <a href="https://www.idesignac.com/heating/">Heating</a>, <a href="https://www.idesignac.com/plumbing/">Plumbing</a>, and <a href="https://www.idesignac.com/electrical-tucson/">Electric</a> for air conditioning services. Our team of certified technicians can provide you with annual maintenance. Getting  seasonal air conditioning services keeps your AC in great working condition. In turn, you will be less likely to have to deal with an AC emergency in the middle of a summer heatwave.</p>
<p>Repairs on a regular basis? If the answer to these questions is yes, then it may be time to buy a new air conditioner</p>
</div>
<div class="section-btn d-inline-block">
                  <a onclick="_scheduler.show({ schedulerId: 'sched_vwgezlwi56yyvwdb0nzlng14' })" type="button" class="clickable-btn btn-blue border-0 st-scheduler-button">Schedule Online Now</a>
               </div>
<div class="section-btn d-inline-block">
                  <a href="tel:+1520-333-2665" class="clickable-btn btn-yellow border-0">Call For A Free Quote</a>
               </div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section class="section-goldilocks section-padding">
<div class="container">
<div class="row align-items-center section-padding-bottom">
<div class="col-lg-6">
<div class="section-img pb-3">
                  <img width="700" height="564" decoding="async" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20700%20564'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="air-conditioning-repair" class="border-radiusfull-10" data-lazy-src="https://www.idesignac.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/ac-condensor-outdoor.jpg"><noscript><img width="700" height="564" decoding="async" src="https://www.idesignac.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/12/ac-condensor-outdoor.jpg" alt="air-conditioning-repair" class="border-radiusfull-10"></noscript>
              </div>
</div>
<div class="col-lg-6">
<div class="section-Content">
<p>In the perfect situation you would set up a maintenance contract as soon as you install a new AC unit. This will guarantee that the unit is always running at top efficiency. It is never too late to take advantage of routine AC maintenance for your existing system. Even if Intelligent Design did not install your AC unit. We can still provide you with annual maintenance with our Family Protection Plans. Springtime is often ideal for air conditioning maintenance.  This way you can be sure to have your air conditioning service before the heat of the summer. You can also set up an annual air conditioning services. That way it is on the books and this checkup doesn’t get overlooked year after year.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="row align-items-center flex-lg-row flex-column-reverse">
<div class="col-lg-6 ps-lg-4">
<div class="section-Content">
<p class="font-18 opensans-600">When you schedule seasonal air conditioning service in Tucson. This is a few key tasks you can expect to take place during the system tune-up:</p>
<ul>
<li>Check thermostat settings.</li>
<li>Check electrical connections and current voltage readings.</li>
<li>Examination of AC components and lubricate moving parts.</li>
<li>Replace air filters.</li>
<li>Remove debris from the area around your outdoor AC unit.</li>
<li>Check condensate drain for clogs and obstructions.</li>
<li>Check refrigerant levels and top of system, if necessary.</li>
</ul>
<p>If your AC is due for annual air conditioning services or you want to set up a maintenance contract. To make sure it stays in great condition. Then call Intelligent Design at <a href="tel:+1520-333-2665">(520) 333-2665</a>. We’re ready to speak with you, so give us a call today!</p>

<div class="row justify-content-center">
<div class="col-lg-10">
<h3 class="text-center text-white"><span id="Why_is_Air_Conditioning_ServicesMaintenance_important">Why is Air Conditioning Services/Maintenance important?</span></h3>
<h6 class="opensans-700 font-18 text-decoration-underline text-white"><span id="HVAC_Repairs_in_Tucson">HVAC Repairs in Tucson</span></h6>
<p class="pb-3">Maintaining your AC has a lot of benefits. First, AC maintenance ensures that you are not overpaying on your home cooling costs. This will keep your unit in peak working condition. Regular maintenance can also lengthen the life of your unit. Finally, AC maintenance can improve the indoor <a class="text-white" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Q-gGvPybITE" target="_blank" rel="noopener">air quality of the home</a>. Here is a closer look at how these benefits can be important to your home.</p>
<h6 class="opensans-700 font-18 text-decoration-underline text-white"><span id="System_Efficiency">System Efficiency</span></h6>
<p class="pb-3">During a tune-up, your HVAC technician will check all components of the AC unit. We do this to make sure that all components are in working order. The technician will also check for any leaks, clogs, or buildups. This can hamper the AC’s cooling capacity. As a result, your AC will work better during peak seasonal use, saving you money on your energy bills. In fact, scheduling an annual maintenance visit could help save you up to 15% on your cooling costs. The biggest benefit is that you will avoid early breakdowns. This way you will be able to get more life out of the current unit.</p>
<h6 class="opensans-700 font-18 text-decoration-underline text-white"><span id="Air_Quality">Air Quality</span></h6>
<p class="pb-3">Another step in the maintenance process is changing the system’s filters. Over time, dust, dirt, and other particulates get into your HVAC system. Filters help to keep these contaminants from recirculating in the system. They will need to swapped out on a set schedule to remain effective.</p>

<h6 class="opensans-700 font-18 text-decoration-underline text-white mb-1"><span id="3_Services_Offered">3. Services Offered</span></h6>

<p class="pb-3">Ensure the company offers a workmanship warranty on their work. This help with providing peace of mind. Look for companies that stand behind their work with a satisfaction guarantee.</p>
<h6 class="opensans-700 font-18 text-decoration-underline text-white mb-1"><span id="6_Pricing_and_Financing">6. Pricing and Financing</span></h6>
<p class="pb-3">Look for a company that provides clear and upfront pricing without hidden fees. If you’re planning a significant investment in a new system. Then be sure to check if the company offers financing options.</p>
<h6 class="opensans-700 font-18 text-decoration-underline text-white mb-1"><span id="7_Customer_Service">7. Customer Service</span></h6>
<p class="pb-3">Choose a company that is responsive and available when you need them. This is especially important for emergency air conditioning services. Look for a company that takes the time to understand your specific needs. Than can also offer personalized solutions base don your needs.</p>

  function _loadHatchScripts(src) {
    try {
      const script = document.createElement("script");
      script.src = src;
      script.async = true;
      script.defer = true;
      script.dataset.hatchid = "67f38a719fd92e00011a4e43"; // Replace with your real Hatch ID
      document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0].parentNode.insertBefore(script, null);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Hatch load error:", err);
    }
  }

  window.hatchChatConfig = {
    autoOpen: false
  };

  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    _loadHatchScripts("https://hatch-javascript.s3.amazonaws.com/hatchChat-app.js");

    // Repeatedly check if hatch-chat is ready and bind click handlers when it is
    const initChatTriggers = () => {
      const hatchEl = document.querySelector("hatch-chat");

      if (hatchEl && hatchEl.shadowRoot) {
        // Hatch is ready: attach click events to all trigger buttons
        const buttons = document.querySelectorAll("#customChatTrigger");
        buttons.forEach(btn => {
          btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
            const openBtn = hatchEl.shadowRoot.querySelector("button#close-pre-engagement");
            if (openBtn) {
              openBtn.click();
            } else {
              console.warn("Open button not found in shadowRoot");
            }
          });
        });
        return; // Stop trying once set
      }

      // Retry every 500ms
      setTimeout(initChatTriggers, 500);
    };

    initChatTriggers();
  });
</script>

    var i, x, tablinks;
    x = document.getElementsByClassName("city");

      x[i].style.display = "none";
    }
    tablinks = document.getElementsByClassName("tablink");
    for (i = 0; i < tablinks.length; i++) {
      tablinks[i].className = tablinks[i].className.replace(" active-tab", "");
    }
    document.getElementById(cityName).style.display = "block";
    evt.currentTarget.className += " active-tab";
